In the quick reply box there is a series of icons at the top. Hover your mouse over each one til you find 'insert image' (Its 3rd from the right end). This will take you to the pictures gallery on your computer, select the photo/image you want, then click 'upload files' and your done. The photo should now be there as 'attachment242' or similar ready for you to post. You will need to add some text to the posting (around 10-15 letters in total) for you  to be able to post.
